<moop> There is a metal bar that runs from each side of the space bar. It's called an equalizer. It's function is to pull down the other side of the space bar when you give it an off center push.Most likely what has happened is that the plastic retainer that holds the bar to the space bar has broken.You could try to gently remove the spacebar by slipping a loop of string under each side and pulling up.
